<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:активизироваться.html>активизи́роваться</a> (28245)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:активизировать.html>активизи́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aktivizírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:действительность.html>действи́тельность</a></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:актуальный.html>актуа́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aktuálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)актуа́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)актуа́льней</b>)

***акула.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:акула.html>аку́ла</a> (9371)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Directly attested since 18th century as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">а́ккула</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ákkula</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акула.html>аку́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akúl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, while derivative <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акулий.html>аку́лий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akulij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used to describe liver oil of a Greenland shark in a source going back to late 16th or early 17th century.
</p><p>Immediate borrowing from rather different <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hákarl</i> (see internal etymology there) is rejected by Anikin, he rather proposes mediation by some <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/S%C3%A1mi_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Sámi languages">Sami</a></span> language.
</p><p>Compare dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">haakall</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Skolt_Sami_language" class="extiw" title="w:Skolt Sami language">Skolt Sami</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sms">akkli</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kildin_S%C3%A1mi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kildin Sámi language">Kildin Sami</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sjd">а̄һклэӈӈк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sjd-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">āhkleŋŋk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_Sami_language" class="extiw" title="w:Northern Sami language">Northern Sami</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="se">áhkạlakkis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Greenland shark</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акула.html>аку́ла</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akúla</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акула.html>аку́лы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акула.html>аку́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акула.html>аку́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shark</li></ol>

***акцент.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:акцент.html>акце́нт</a> (4997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акцент.html>акце́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akcént</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акцент.html>акце́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акцент.html>акце́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акцент.html>акце́нтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(grammar)</i> stress, accent</li>
<li>accent <i>(foreign or local)</i>

***акция.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кция</a> (2250)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ákcija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> share, stock
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привилегированный.html>привилегиро́ванные</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кции</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">privilegiróvannyje <b>ákcii</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">preferred <b>stock</b></span></div></dd>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> diplomacy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> action, move, demarche
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кция</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:протест.html>проте́ста</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ákcija</b> protésta</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>protest</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vojénnaja <b>ákcija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">military <b>action</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">marketing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> promotion, campaign; special offer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рекламный.html>рекла́мная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">reklámnaja <b>ákcija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">advertising <b>campaign</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>organized public event
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благотворительный.html>благотвори́тельная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:акция.html>а́кция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">blagotvorítelʹnaja <b>ákcija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">charity <b>event</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:албанский.html>алба́нский</a> (26115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">алба́ния</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Albánija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:албанский.html>алба́нский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">albánskij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:албанский.html>алба́нского</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Albanian language</li>
<li>an online slang based on intentional misspelling of the Russian language</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:албанский.html>алба́нский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">albánskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Albanian</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">

***алгоритм.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:алгоритм.html>алгори́тм</a> (21161)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">algorithme</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">algorismus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">الخُوَارِزْمِيّ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">al-ḵuwārizmiyy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the nisba of Persian mathematician <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muhammad_ibn_Musa_al-Khwarizmi" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Muhammad ibn Musa al-Khwarizmi">Muhammad ibn Musa Al-Khwarizmi</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">александри́я</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Aleksandríja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́йский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íjskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> when referring to Alexandria; from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">алекса́ндр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Aleksándr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́йский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íjskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> when referring to Alexander the Great.

***алкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:алкать.html>алка́ть</a> (28658)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">алъкати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">alŭkati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*olkati</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лакать.html>лака́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lakátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:алкать.html>алка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">alkátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to crave, to thirst (for), to be greedy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Preserved in modern Russian as the present tense active participle <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:алкать.html>а́лчущий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">álčuščij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hungry, craving, greedy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (of conjugation pattern "6a").</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаждать.html>жа́ждать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žáždatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взалка́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vzalkátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:алчность.html>а́лчность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">álčnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
